ss=3D"row"><div class=3D"small-12 medium-11 medium-centered columns"><h1 cl=
ass=3D"display-lg">Our Story</h1><p>In 1999, our founder, Dave Bolotsky, vi=
sited a craft show and was inspired to build something that had never exist=
ed before: an online marketplace to connect makers and their creations with=
 shoppers looking for truly unique goods.</p><p>Over the last 26 years, we=
=92ve grown to approximately 150 year-round team members with thousands of =
packages heading from our home in Brooklyn to customers across the country =
each day.</p></div></div></div></div><div class=3D"row"><div class=3D"small=
-4 small-centered columns"><hr class=3D"decoration margin-lg"></div></div><=
div class=3D"row"><div class=3D"small-12 medium-10 large-8 small-centered c=
olumns text-center"><blockquote class=3D"margin-lg"><p>Uncommon Goods is my=
 first stop for gift shopping. Thanks for scouring the planet to find these=
 little gems for us, and for being the kind of company I can feel good abou=
t supporting.</p><footer><cite>a happy customer</cite></footer></blockquote=
></div></div><div class=3D"row"><div class=3D"small-12 medium-6 medium-push=
-6 columns"><h2>Our Products</h2><p>Our collection has grown from Dave's cr=
aft show finds to thousands of designs handpicked by our buying team, who s=
earch all year for unique goods from around the world. We also discover uni=
que pieces through online submissions from our community of artists and des=
igners. Thanks to our in-house product development team, we create our own =
goods, too.</p><p>Every design we carry incorporates elements of creativity=
. We look for goods that:</p><ul><li><p>Serve a purpose</p></li><li><p>Solv=
e a problem</p></li><li><p>Stun us with their beauty</p></li><li><p>Are han=
dmade with exceptional craft and skill</p></li><li><p>Use unusual, reclaime=
d, or recycled materials</p></li><li><p>Are made without leather, feathers,=
 or fur</p></li><li><p>Make us wonder, =93Why hasn't anyone thought of this=
 before?=94</p></li></ul></div><div class=3D"small-12 medium-6 medium-pull-=
6 columns text-center"><div class=3D"even-grid small-2-across grid-gap-sm m=

g it, and the process that leads to the finished design. From potters to pa=
inters to jewelry artists to craftspeople of all kinds, we've worked with h=
undreds of makers over the years. We're proud to offer independent designer=
s a place to showcase their work.</p></div><div class=3D"small-12 medium-6 =

ass=3D"small-12 medium-6 columns"><h2>Founding B Corporation</h2><p>In 2007=
, we became a founding member of an alliance of companies committed to usin=
g business as a force for good. By passing an in-depth screening, we offici=
ally became one of the first B Corporations. We're driven to continuously e=
valuate and improve ourselves, while spreading the word about certification=
. To date, more than 8,500 companies including Patagonia, Ben &amp; Jerry=
=92s, Allbirds, and King Arthur Baking Company have joined the B Corp commu=
nity.</p><p>How did we earn this score, and what exactly does it mean? Visi=
t our <a href=3D"https://www.bcorporation.net/en-us/find-a-b-corp/company/u=
ncommongoods" target=3D"_blank" rel=3D"noopener">B Corp profile</a> to lear=
n more.</p></div><div class=3D"small-12 medium-6 columns"><any-picture><pic=
